               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Butterfly Face Painting/Makeup Artists
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Dear friends, fellow painters and members, I have thought about some things brought to my attention concerning these groups! 1. Firstly, I had originally made these groups for one reason only - to let all of us quickly access photos to use for ideas, inspiration &amp; preparation for events and gigs, to share and use for practice; all in one place to eliminate time spent searching for that one great pic, but couldn't remember where it was last seen. 2. To keep photos &amp; ideas of a specific theme in one location for ease of access. 3. Please, no advertising. We have enough groups through which this can be done. Lastly, for now, after a little research I think that open groups are better for what we have in mind, they can be found quickly and used by all interested in one specific theme. I want all to benefit from having so many photos all in one place! Thank you very much for understanding!
                </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 SoCal Historic Architecture
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This page is a celebration of Southern California's amazing historic architecture. Feel free to post pictures (with descriptions) and comments! (But please, nothing commercial.) And be nice! Regarding what constitutes historic architecture: An historic building is generally considered to be a building or structure that has some kind of 'historic value', i.e. people in the present are connected to it via past events in some way. This value warrants it being afforded consideration in planning decisions that have to be made concerning it. A building may hold special historic interest because of its importance with respect to a particular historical event or period, or be associated with nationally important people. Alternatively, there might be special historic interest in the building itself, i.e. its construction methods, design, architectural significance, and so on. In this instance the building does not have to be older than 50 years as is generally a consideration for landmark. 
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">1.2&nbsp;万位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">9 篇新帖</span></span>
                </div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 A Passion For Art
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Goals and Rules: The goal of A Passion for Art is to share good quality art. Feel free to submit your paintings and drawings for approval, and to invite your friends by sharing this page. We'd like to ensure professional artists, students, and dabblers have the opportunity to share their completed work. Occasionally we select an artist to pin to the top of the page to highlight great work. Page rules: - No excessive watermarks. - Absolutely no porn. - No photography. - No tattoos or bodyart. - No cartoons, manga, superheroes, or horror. - No links to exhibitions or competitions, lessons, or classes. - No crafts, including jewelry, mosaics, pottery, woodworking, or sculpture. - Since we have 20,000+ members, we ask that you share your finished piece only once, and please limit submissions to 4-5 photos at one time. Unfortunately, FB doesn't let admin reject just one in a group, so all will end up being rejected. - Videos are fine if they show a work in progress to completion, or the recent case of a memorial tribute to a group of young artists. - Links to your art page in FB or your website are fine. Works for sale are fine. - If you submit artwork for someone other than yourself, we assume that you have permission to do so. Thanks for sharing your artwork and for helping build an online community in support of fine art. 
                </div>
               </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 3D REALISTIC
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 3D Realistic Group es una comunidad abierta a todo el mundo, no importando su procedencia, nacionalidad, raza, sexo, ideología, ya sea religiosa o política, y que fue creada con el fin de reunir estudiantes, arquitectos y/o personas interesadas en la rama del Diseño 3D, con el objetivo de conversar, discutir e intercambiar experiencias y conocimientos con todos los temas relacionados con la profesión. El Grupo tiene, como todo buen servicio abierto al público, una administración y una moderación que velarán por mantener el orden, la paz y la tranquilidad de todos los usuarios que participen en el. "EVITEMOS" No esta permitido la solicitud, o promoción de contenido pirata. Por lo tanto serán borrados. Si observas algún post donde encuentras algún tema de este tipo. REPORTALO. El Grupo no se responsabiliza por el contenido y origen de los aportes realizados por los usuarios. Ante cualquier duda dirigirte a los administradores del Grupo. Para evitar que los Administradores, edite o borre los temas en los que participas te recomendamos seguir los siguientes consejos: Las preguntas que hagas, como así también las respuestas deben ser respetuosas de los otros miembros del Grupo, y estar en un marco de solidaridad y amistad. No escribas todo tu post con mayúsculas interpretamos eso como un grito o exaltación. No insultes a los demás miembros de la comunidad, por el simple hecho de que no compartas su opinión, a pesar de que en esta comunidad apoyamos la libertad de expresión, si vemos que una discusión se convierte en riña llena de insultos, la discusión será borrada. Procura no usar malas palabras, es muy seguro que el habrá reportes de tu conducta, te pedimos esto por que al tratarse de un Grupo numeroso, es visitado por personas con todo tipo de criterios. www.3drealistic.net 
                </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 sculpture
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Sculpture is three-dimensional art made by one of four basic processes. The earliest known human artefacts recognisable as what we would call sculpture date from the period known as the Upper Paleolithic, which is roughly from 40,000 to 10,000 years ago. At that time, as well as making carved sculpture, the Greeks brought the technique of casting sculpture in bronze to a high degree of sophistication. Following the fall of the Roman Empire the technique of bronze casting was almost lost but, together with carved sculpture, underwent a major revival at the Renaissance. I
                </div>

                 Here you can post and share your art, this way, hopefully, we can support each other. Please visit www.sublimepaintings.com IMPORTANT TO READ BEFORE ANY POST! -----If you wish to post your link's website, please make sure you attach at least one of your artwork of any kind. Otherwise, spamming posts with just your link will get banned from this group. ------Please, don't post any sexually explicit content, this is an art group and also we have young audience. Doing so, will get your posts banned from this group. ------Spamming post, games, politics, social network generator of Facebook and all other subjects non-related to art, are not allowed. Please, don’t insult other members! Posting is open for people genuinely interested in participating and promoting their art, within reason and at the discretion of this group's administrator. It is hard, frustrating, knowing that you can't share with anyone your art and it is impossible to get noticed (of course, before all, we all know that it is your talent, but without "marketing", it is not that easy to be noticed). It is not just me convinced that in this world there are valuable artists, undiscovered, that will never get attention. Welcome and enjoy the group and making new, valuable, friends!

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Art Opportunities, Jobs, and Advice
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 **Rules: This group is for sharing VISUAL ART opportunities, jobs, and advice. Because of the very high numbers of requests to join the group, members will only be added if their FB profiles show their involvement in art. They will be accepted once a month. When posting: - state the location of the opportunity or job (this group is international) - include any location requirements or restrictions and any fees involved - verify all links (URLs) Posts Allowed: - opportunities for studio space - opportunities for jobs in the arts - opportunities for jobs that may help visual artists - opportunities for awards for visual artists: grants, residencies, fellowships, etc. - educational events, like workshops or seminars, that specifically offer artists opportunities, jobs, or advice - requests for advice on visual-arts materials, techniques, methods, approaches - requests for advice on business and career strategies and protocols in the art world, particularly for visual artists Posts Not Allowed: - general announcements for art exhibitions and events - announcements that publicize or promote your or someone else’s art, website, exhibitions, performances, screenings, blogs, events, etc. - requests for donations to crowd-funding campaigns, for votes in contests, for signatures on petitions, for FB page “likes”, or for participation in surveys - announcements of unpaid internships. Any posted internship opportunity must state the compensation for the intern (e.g., studio space, stipend, transit expenses---“experience" is not sufficient). If you have a business that offers services to artists, please share but clearly state your connection to that business. If you are being harassed: Take a screenshot of the offending post; do not respond to it; flag any harassing comments to alert the administrators (Click the three dots at the top right of the post and select Report Post to Group Admins.) If a post doesn't apply to this group, it will be deleted. If you do not follow the rules, you will be removed from the group. If you are unsure about anything, send a message to ask an administrator. Disagreements are fine, but mutual respect is essential. Members who display negativity or are deemed offensive will be removed from the group. 
                </div>

                 Welcome... Group guidelines... This is a group to share our love of graffiti and street art and all that relates to it, from paper to canvas to wall, all skill levels, its all welcome. Please only post pics that are graffiti or closely related, fine art, portraits and tattoo designs and such are welcomed in other groups that don't allow graff. Please only post decent quality pics posted the correct way up (if they are sideways they will be deleted) ...so to keep a certain amount of quality in the newsfeed. Have fun and be nice. Peace

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 PLEASE READ. Welcome to one of the fastest growing art communities on social media. A group designated to be a virtual ART GALLERY for artistic endeavors, art lovers, curators enthusiasts and buyers. Members worldwide can view your art. We're primarily an acrylic painting group. (Censorship is on a limited basis, This is an adult group however please use discretion, common sense &amp; respect one another ) Avoid being oust by following the community GUIDELINES: • NO trolling, bullying, spammers or rudeness • If you're easily offended by NUDES you probably don't belong here • SELL ART ONLY. If it's not art related, it doesn't belong here • Acrylic on canvas is the primary focus of this group • Images focusing on genitals or intercourse is forbidden • The focus of this page is original art. Don't post any work and or try to sell copyright material to which you do not own the rights to. This is considered copyright© infringement and protected by law. • Police yourselves: Someone gets nasty on your thread hide &amp; block them • This page belongs to us all. Please be vigilant of any unusual postings and activities. REPORT IMMEDIATELY. • Images &amp; or members could be removed at any given time Before posting a question on the page, please use the “Search this group” field in the left-hand nav bar. Many questions, on subjects about materials, technique, and selling your work have been asked dozens of times and you can find answers there. Simply type in your subject, like “gesso,” “varnish,” “prints,” etc.' THANK YOU for making this a Great Group!!! https://www.facebook.com/BenCasiano/

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ------------------------------------------------------------------------ Welcome to the review group! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ May the Architect be High Minded not arrogant but Faithful Just and easy to deal with, without avarice, Not let his mind be occupied in receiving gifts But let him preserve his good name with Dignity. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ -Daig ng Preparado ang Matalino -If u Fail to Plan, You are Planning to Fail -di mahirap ang Board exam, tao lang gumawa ng questions, kaya, kaya rin sagutan ng tao ang mga questions. ^_^ tara! Review Tayo! ------------------------------------------------------------------------- Feel Free to post, ask, suggest, teach, share to the group,,, Share your knowledge and concerns to others, be Blessed and be a Blessing to many... God bless PLEASE DO NOT POST NON ARCHITECTURE RELATED TOPIC/ POST ADVERTISEMENT IN THIS GROUP, anything that is non-beneficial to the profession will be deleted. posting and spamming of these post maybe banned permanently to the group without prior notice, ---------------------------------------------------------------------------- Dear members, Please be advise that you are free to post review questions here as many as you like, and be also informed that posting such will give you the responsibility to give the CORRECT/BEST answer to the questions you post. You may give the answer after many or more than 2 have given their answer. Be also aware &amp;responsible not to mislead others w/ your answer and explanations. Don't forget to press like to the correct/best answer/comment as possible. In posting review questions, suggestions, facts, discussions &amp; alike, you may also put the source if possible to acknowledge them. Be blessed and be a blessing. Thank you. -by admin

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Tattoo Conventions
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Tattoo Conventions! Post your tattoo convention news, dates, event info, travels, photos of tattoos from conventions and any other convention info you'd like to share with the tattoo industry and community. Every weekend of every month there are tattoo conventions all around the world. These gatherings that celebrate body art consist of tattoo artists, collectors and enthusiasts from around the globe coming together from around the world to show their tattoo work and give people a place to come, watch and also get tattooed! Share your Tattoo Conventions here! Please do not SPAM this with ANY non-convention related material. Failure to follow these rules will have your post deleted from the group or possible ban.

Whether it's yours or not(just give credit where credits due). It's all about the culture. Finally all other forms of art will be allowed and not discriminated on. So if this is a issue then this group just might not be for you!!!

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 California "Rocks" on Facebook
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 󾠄We paint rocks to "hide in the open " around California to spread joy and brighten people's day, come join us! This is a state building group meant to inspire creativity in all ages and energize people to explore our state . All you have to do is find some rocks and some painting supplies or markers and get creative! We do ask that you keep the artwork PG rated to ensure fun for all ages. We would appreciate on the back of your rock if you'd reference our page California "Rocks" on Facebook Make sure to seal your rocks ( if raining ) before placing them outside. We would love you to post photos of your rocks before you hide them, or when you find them, but you can participate anonymously if you'd like. If you find a rock you are welcome to keep it or re-hide it for someone else to find. If you decide to keep a rock we would like to encourage you to paint and hide some of your own (but, of course, this is optional). The goal is to get lots of people all across our communities and state painting so that there are lots of rocks to be found out there. You might find yourself rediscovering parts of your community and state you haven't appreciated in a while. Get out and ENJOY ! Add any of your friends to our group who would be interested in doing this and share the link to this group on your personal FB page. *Please be careful to where you hide your rocks to not cause damage to property. Don't steal rocks from people's landscaping. *You can hint to where you're hiding your rocks *Painted rocks reflect the opinions, attitudes, and creative expressions of the individual artist and not those of the page admin. We cannot be held responsible if you are offended. Make sure you write on the back of the rock California "Rocks"s on Facebook 󾠄
                </div>

All Theatre Chat groups can be used in emergencies. Theatre Chat groups have been used in Earth Quakes, Hurricanes, Tornados, Fires and even Pandemics to help inform fellow members. PLEASE NOTE: There are a few of our groups that may fit your specific needs, by sharing arts to TARGET AUDIENCES, by CITY or STATE, NATIONALLY and GLOBALLY. BROADWAYGLOBAL.ORG group is for global arts news. INTERNATIONAL THEATRE CHAT is also for global arts news. WEST END THEATRE CHAT is for that specific area. USA THEATRE CHAT is for national tours or national arts news. With over 30 city/state Theatre Chat groups each group allows members to focus on target audiences by specific locations. Our Theatre Chat groups are core of the arts movement! Please share arts links/info that keep artists employed and patrons informed. USA THEATRE CHAT, NYC THEATRE CHAT, WAS DC AREA, FLORIDA THEATRE CHAT, CHICAGO THEATRE CHAT, OHIO THEATRE CHAT, LOS ANGELES THEATRE CHAT, SAN FRANCISCO/ BAY AREA THEATRE CHAT... This are just a few of our groups. We remind all members to be transparent, offering a phone and website with a business address is best for the safety of all members. All members should go to original sources to verify creditability. Cameron's Theatre Chat and past examiner (.com) articles have featured conversations with Tony Award winning Broadway Producer Stewart Lane, Emmy Award winning Casting Director Jeff Greenberg, multiple Broadway and TV stars and creative teams bringing arts lovers together around the world for the largest social media arts movement. Tag You're it! Please Subscribe and share with your arts community. Post your press releases, auditions, show promo pictures/video via Theatre Chat and reach thousands of local, national and international Theatre Chat members. Show info and auditions should come from the original source. We do not allow sign up sites, email news letter links, You Tube self promotion videos, blogs, or casting sites without the original source. Phone and website with a business address is safest for all Theatre Chat members. Feel free to contact Admin Richard Cameron by email or phone should you have questions.                  This group is for beginners, beyonders, and everyone in between. 🎨 We have weekly painting challenges, most with a prize! (Winners chosen randomly). Be kind to others. Whether you want to learn more, or just share your watercolor paintings for others to enjoy, come on in. 🙂

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Architecture is a noble profession. Through this forum we are trying to keep the creative and inspirational fire burning among our group members. Here, a Young Architect/ architectural student may get work, thesis guidance, new ideas or read about the latest from famous architects. One may also come across articles and works of past Masters. One can also feel inspired by the photos/details of the current architectural projects going on around the world, just to rejuvenate their own creativity.We aim to break the distance between different architectural styles practiced all over the world. Foremost of all, this forum aims to provide a platform for networking of all Architects/ students/ job seekers and prospective clients or like-minded professionals.......

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Burlesque Hall of Fame
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to The Burlesque Hall of Fame Group, a gathering place and resource for people interested in our mission to preserve, share, celebrate, and inspire the art of burlesque. Paid membership in The Burlesque Hall of Fame is not required, but it is WHOLEHEARTEDLY encouraged. This group is for sharing and discussing topics related to burlesque and The Burlesque Hall of Fame. We are committed to providing a safe and open space for conversation on subjects that matter to us as members of the burlesque community and/or fans of the museum. In order to best meet this goal, we ask that you abide by the following guidelines: - All posts must be somehow related to either burlesque or to BHoF. There are plenty of forums on Facebook for discussing other matters, so no matter how important the topic may be, posts addressing subjects that are not clearly burlesque-related will be deleted. - We honor diversity of opinion and welcome respectful disagreement. Personal insults and language disparaging a racial, ethnic, gender, sexual orientation, nationality, age, and/or disability group are not ”respectful” and will be deleted. Repeated use of such language will lead to the member being banned. - This is not a “secret” group but please do not repost content from this group without the author’s permission. - Banning a moderator or administrator or refusing to heed warnings by a moderator or administrator will result in removal from the group. - Please limit ad postings and self-promotion. If your primary posting here is promotional, you will be snoozed and eventually removed from the group. - We welcome photos but please limit photo posts to one per day maximum. If you would like to post more than one photo, please post them together as a single post. We are here to celebrate the people who created and continue to create the burlesque artform. This is first and foremost a woman-positive and sexuality-positive space. Please do your best to make sure your contributions here are aimed at that fundamental goal. 
                </div>
               </div>

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 GROUP RULES -Welcome! This is a group to promote and support the VISUAL ARTS. All artists and students, amateurs, novices, and professionals are invited to join, connect, and network, learn, share, and have fun. People who are not artists, but who enjoy and appreciate visual art, are also welcome. We ask our members to be respectful and polite toward others. No profanity, hateful speech, or other behavior that is offensive. This is a community of individuals, with the common goal of being supportive, positive and nurturing toward our fellow creative people. GROUP RULES -GUIDELINES FOR POSTING AND COMMENTING IN THIS GROUP Please read this document published under the FILES tab of our group. It covers everything you need to know about how to participate in the group for your best experience. You may send personal messages to the group owner with any questions about group policies. https://www.facebook.com/notes/262733959248/GUIDELINES:%20RULES%20FOR%20POSTING%20AND%20COMMENTING%20IN%20THIS%20GROUP/10153540988484249/ We wish you all success and prosperity! Thank you very much. Sarah Dees, Administrator, group owner Cari Anne Robaldo, Administrator Chih Min Chan - Administrator Angela Freeman, Moderator Jennifer Wilson, Moderator Dorothy-Chris Arrington-Humphries Moderator Christie Shinn, Moderator Jorge Camacho - Moderator Holly Pawson - Moderator Valentine Louafi - Moderator Angie Adkins - Moderator Travis Patterson - Moderator David Thomas - Moderator Jaroid Henry - Moderator John Morris - Moderator

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Bauhaus Art
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The Bauhaus was founded by Walter Gropius in Weimar. The German term Bauhaus literally "construction house" was understood as meaning "School of Building", but in spite of its name and the fact that its founder was an architect, the Bauhaus did not have an architecture department during its first years of existence. Nonetheless, it was founded with the idea of creating a "total" work of art (Gesamtkunstwerk) in which all arts, including architecture, would eventually be brought together. The Bauhaus style later became one of the most influential currents in modern design, Modernist architecture and art, design and architectural education. The Bauhaus had a profound influence upon subsequent developments in art, architecture, graphic design, interior design, industrial design, and typography.
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">5.4&nbsp;万位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">3 篇新帖</span></span>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Hamilton American Musical Fans
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  Hamilton is a musical about the life of American Founding Father Alexander Hamilton, with music, lyrics and book by Lin-Manuel Miranda.[1] The show, inspired by the 2004 biography Alexander Hamilton by historian Ron Chernow, achieved both critical acclaim and box office success. The musical made its Off-Broadway debut at The Public Theater in February 2015, where its engagement was sold out.[2] The show transferred to Broadway in August 2015 at the Richard Rodgers Theatre. On Broadway, it received enthusiastic critical acclaim and unprecedented advance box office sales.[3] Nominated for a record-setting 16 Tony Awards, the production ultimately won 11, including Best Musical, and is also the recipient of the 2016 Grammy Award for Best Musical Theater Album and the 2016 Pulitzer Prize for Drama. The prior off-Broadway production of Hamilton won the 2015 Drama Desk Award for Outstanding Musical as well as seven other Drama Desk Awards out of 14 total nominated categories. 
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Art Deco
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 I love Art Deco / J'aime l'Art Déco ________________________________________ Art Deco was a popular international art design movement from 1925 until 1939, affecting the decorative arts such as architecture, interior design, and industrial design, as well as the visual arts such as fashion, painting, the graphic arts and film. At the time, this style was seen as elegant, glamorous, functional, and modern. The movement was a mix of many different styles and movements of the early 20th century, including Neoclassical, Constructivism, Cubism, Modernism, Art Nouveau, and Futurism. Its popularity peaked in Europe during the Roaring Twenties and continued strongly in the United States through the 1930s. Although many design movements have political or philosophical roots or intentions, Art Deco was purely decorative. Art Deco experienced a decline in popularity during the late 30s and early 40s, and soon fell out of public favor. It experienced a resurgence with the popularization of graphic design in the 1980s. Art Deco had a profound influence on many later artistic movements, such as Memphis and Pop art. Share with us your photos, websites, or anything concerning art deco or things that match with it! ________________________________________ De 1920 à 1939, et en réaction à l'Art nouveau d'avant la Première Guerre mondiale, l'Art déco fut un mouvement artistique extrêmement influent surtout dans l'architecture et le design, mais concerna en fait plus ou moins toutes les formes d'arts plastiques. Le style Art déco tire son nom de l'Exposition internationale des Arts Décoratifs et industriels modernes qui se tint à Paris en 1925. Partagez vos coups de cœur, vos photos, les sites Internet, ou quoi que ce soit d’autre concernant l’art déco (et autre) !
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">3.5&nbsp;万位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">14 篇新帖</span></span>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Hamilton The Musical Fans
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 It might be nice... It might be nice... to have other fans on your side Every action has its equal opposite reaction. Now that I love Hamilton, I wanted a place for fandom interaction. I looked and asked for a group of fans or maybe to form our own new faction. But all I could find was a lack of impactful pages, not up to my satisfaction. Thought Hamilton fans would’ve already planned a group, and it'd be gaining traction. There’s too many passionate fans to ration a page like this wouldn’t have an attraction. I searched all over Facebook, but alas, thus far, results didn't match. So this page is a space to engage and discuss if it's something that Hamilton fandom has lacked. A group should exist with no need for permission to go if you're wishing to post and submit, and- I was happy rise up to tackle the task if a lyricist needed to fill the position. I don’t want to clash or begin a new rift. My suspicion is others had similar visions So I insisted to listen to anyone with information and resist to create a new page until it was explicit and I was convinced this ambition is not in existence, now this group is out There are Ten Group Commandments. Other than that, friends- I'll leave you to it...

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Painting Best Practices
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The choices that artists make of painting materials and techniques have consequences on the longevity of their work. This group is a discussion about those choices and how our present understanding of these materials and techniques from conservation research and practice can help artists make better choices. Please follow all group rules and do not post self-promotions and images of your paintings (unless there is a question or example about the materials or techniques used in the painting). Please research your answers before posting comments. Group Moderators will delete posts that contain information that does not conform to best practices in painting. The purpose of this group is helping people, and providing wrong advice does not fit that objective. Posts will be deleted at the sole discretion of the group's Moderators. Anyone whose posts are deleted may be placed on Moderator Approval for all new posts. If you are unsure your comment is accurate, please don't post it. Do your research in the group or from external resources. Among the members of this group are experts in the conservation and materials fields who can provide reliable information based on education, training, and experience, so questions can be answered correctly with sound advice. Painting Best Practices is an information-packed workshop includes all aspects of constructing a painting from the support and ground to the final layers. Practical procedures are clearly explained and demonstrated on how to build paintings based on conservation research during the past century. This workshop is designed for painters of all mediums, but special emphasis is given to oil painting. For more information on the Painting Best Practices workshop, please visit: https://www.naturalpigments.com/artist-materials/painting-best-practices
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Deconstruction Architecture
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Deconstruction Architecture is not just a movement or architectural model is indefinite appeared on the horizon in 1971 It is a major cultural phenomenon of the most significant developments in modern art and architecture in the current era It Is the method of monetary and philosophical style *Deconstructivism ideas are borrowed from the F[r]ench philosopher Jacques Derrida. - its astronauts: --Franko Gehry --Z.Hadid --Peter Eisenman --Rem Koolhass --B.Tschumi --Daniel Libeskind its Philosophy : --The discrepancy between the form of the building and the land it. --Discrepancies between traditional structure installation and decoration. --Deconstruction calls to demolish all the bases engineering Alakulaidsih. --Calls to reconsider the relations whether humanitarian or physical. --Rights are linked roles as child dismantle the game and radio eagerly to know its contents and how it works. --This could be attained delightful basic instincts of man. ---&gt;Deconstructivism, or Deconstruction, is an approach to building design which attempts to view architecture in bits and pieces. The basic elements of architecture are dismantled. Deconstructivist buildings may seem to have no visual logic: They may appear to be made up of unrelated, disharmonious abstract forms. 
                </div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Historical Timber Framing, Traditional Building and Architecture Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 A friendly discussion group for folks interested in timber framing and ALL types of historical architecture, details, construction, techniques, and materials. We welcome all topics related to building before roughly 1880, when traditional building practices for millenia began to change over to the modern. Environmental protection and awareness of endangered natural resources, is crucial to the plight of the traditional craftsperson and our professions. So too is the discussion of historical preservation against ignorance and destruction. We encourage questions, discussions and content, pictures etc, of all people, young or old, experienced or newbie, regardless of sex gender religion or ethnicity. We are adults- play nice. There is 0 tolerance for racism sexism, ethnocentrism, mean spirited baiting here. If you have a question or complaint you can message me or any of the moderators. cheers ! Drew Young www.ChesapeakeArtistry.com www.HistoryMovers.org 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 We Love Pro Wrestling
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Here is a short version of the rules. Please read them. For the full rules, please click the link at the bottom. 1. All threads must be related to professional wrestling 2. Any threats will result in an immediate ban 3. There is a zero tolerance policy with regard to racist, homophobic, sexist, offensive, and insulting comments 4. No flaming/trolling - "Having fun is fine, just don't go overboard”; If you are warned by an Admin with regard to specific comments, please defer to the discretion of that Admin. 5. Any direct attacks or negative public statements directed towards the Admin Team will result in immediate and permanent removal from the group 6. No unauthorized advertising 7. All Facebook rules apply in this group 8. The Admin staff reserves the right to delete any and all threads 9. Contact the admin team if you would like to see a “Top____” threads 10. Please check for duplicate/similar posts before posting to avoid clutter 11. No spam posting. This includes pictures and posts. 12. Please answer a topic with an answer that fits the question. 13. Look before you post. We know that having over 80k members is a lot. Look before posting “Breaking News” because there is a good chance someone beat you to the punch 14. If your thread was removed, it was either a duplicate thread or inappropriate. It will not be reposted. 15. You can discuss Chris Benoit all you want, but it's based only on his career. Nothing else. 16. If you see anyone spamming, selling glasses, sneakers or anything else you believe shouldn’t be. Mark the thread as spam. Doing so will alert the Admin team and we will look into the post. 17. Refrain from using words that go beyond a PG-13 rating. If you need to think about it, don't use the word. Any language considered over the line will be deleted on sight, and possible removal from the group could result. 18. The exit is always open. No one here is forcing you to stay at WLPW; if you do not like or agree with the way things are being run here, please leave. 19. Grammar. We realize that English is not everyone’s first language. However, we ask that the wording of the post at least makes sense. 20. All posts will not go through without Admin approval. This is to make it easier to weed out duplicate posts, spam, bots and spoilers. This is especially true during peak times such as RAW, SmackDown! And pay-per-views. Full rules can be found here: https://www.facebook.com/notes/we-love-pro-wrestling/we-love-pro-wrestling-rules-and-regulations/452741174913554/ Manage 
                </div>
               </div>

𝗔 𝗺𝗲𝗺𝗯𝗲𝗿 𝗰𝗮𝗻 𝗽𝗼𝘀𝘁 2 𝗣𝗼𝘀𝘁𝘀 𝗽𝗲𝗿 𝗱𝗮𝘆. 𝟮. 𝗙𝗕 𝗽𝗮𝗴𝗲 𝗹𝗶𝗻𝗸, 𝗪𝗲𝗯𝘀𝗶𝘁𝗲 𝗹𝗶𝗻𝗸, 𝗬𝗼𝘂𝗧𝘂𝗯𝗲 𝗹𝗶𝗻𝗸𝘀 𝗮𝗿𝗲 𝗮𝗹𝗹𝗼𝘄𝗲𝗱 𝘄𝗶𝘁𝗵 𝘆𝗼𝘂𝗿 𝗿𝗲𝗴𝘂𝗹𝗮𝗿 𝗽𝗼𝘀𝘁𝘀. 𝟯. 𝗢𝗻𝗹𝘆 𝗜𝗻𝘁𝗲𝗿𝗶𝗼𝗿, 𝗔𝗿𝗰𝗵𝗶𝘁𝗲𝗰𝘁𝘂𝗿𝗲 &amp; 𝗵𝗼𝗺𝗲 𝗱𝗲𝗰𝗼𝗿𝗮𝘁𝗶𝗼𝗻 𝗿𝗲𝗹𝗮𝘁𝗲𝗱 𝗽𝗼𝘀𝘁𝘀 𝗮𝗿𝗲 𝗮𝗹𝗹𝗼𝘄𝗲𝗱. 𝑫𝒊𝒔𝒂𝒍𝒍𝒐𝒘𝒆𝒅 : 1. 𝗗𝗼 𝗻𝗼𝘁 𝗽𝗼𝘀𝘁𝘀 𝗮𝗯𝗼𝘂𝘁 𝗮𝗻𝘆 F𝗲𝘀𝘁𝗶𝘃𝗮𝗹 𝗼𝗿 P𝘂𝗯𝗹𝗶𝗰 𝗵𝗼𝗹𝗶𝗱𝗮𝘆𝘀. 2. 𝗦𝗮𝘆 𝗡𝗢 𝘁𝗼 𝗽𝗼𝗹𝗶𝘁𝗶𝗰𝘀 𝗮𝗻𝗱 𝗿𝗲𝗹𝗶𝗴𝗶𝗼𝘂𝘀 𝗽𝗼𝘀𝘁𝘀. 3. 𝗦𝗮𝘆 𝗡𝗢 𝘁𝗼 𝗵𝗮𝘁𝗲 𝗰𝗼𝗺𝗺𝗲𝗻𝘁𝘀 &amp; 𝘀𝗰𝗮𝗺𝗺𝗶𝗻𝗴. 𝟰. 𝗜𝗻 𝗰𝗮𝘀𝗲 𝗮 𝗺𝗲𝗺𝗯𝗲𝗿 𝗰𝗼𝗺𝗽𝗹𝗮𝗶𝗻𝘁𝘀 𝘁𝗵𝗮𝘁 𝘆𝗼𝘂 𝗮𝗿𝗲 𝗺𝗶𝘀𝘂𝘀𝗶𝗻𝗴 𝘁𝗵𝗲𝗶𝗿 𝗰𝗼𝗽𝘆𝗿𝗶𝗴𝗵𝘁 𝗽𝗵𝗼𝘁𝗼𝘀, 𝗼𝘄𝗻 𝘄𝗿𝗶𝘁𝗶𝗻𝗴𝘀 𝗼𝗿 𝗰𝗮𝗽𝘁𝗶𝗼𝗻𝘀 &amp; 𝗙𝗯 𝗣𝗮𝗴𝗲 𝗹𝗮𝘆𝗼𝘂𝘁 𝘁𝗵𝗲𝗻 𝘆𝗼𝘂 𝘄𝗶𝗹𝗹 𝗯𝗲 𝗽𝗲𝗿𝗺𝗮𝗻𝗲𝗻𝘁𝗹𝘆 𝗯𝗹𝗼𝗰𝗸𝗲𝗱 𝗶𝗻𝗰𝗹𝘂𝗱𝗶𝗻𝗴 𝗮𝗹𝗹 𝘆𝗼𝘂𝗿 𝗜𝗗❜𝘀 𝘄𝗵𝗶𝗰𝗵 𝘆𝗼𝘂 𝘂𝘀𝗲 𝘁𝗼 𝗽𝗼𝘀𝘁 𝗶𝗻 𝗼𝘂𝗿 𝗚𝗿𝗼𝘂𝗽.               <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Vietnam Art Space
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Vietnam Art Space (VAS) được tạm dịch là Không Gian Nghệ Thuật Việt Nam là cầu nối mang các hoạ sỹ và người yêu nghệ thuật được tiếp cận gần hơn với hội họa mỹ thuật mang bản sắc Việt, do người Việt sáng tạo làm nên. VAS là nơi các họa sỹ có thể giao lưu, chia sẻ, kết nối, học hỏi, kết bạn với những người Việt có cùng sở thích hội họa khắp mọi nơi trên thế giới. Nơi bạn có thể ngắm nhìn các tác phẩm đẹp làm bạn rung động, đẩy bạn có hứng khởi sáng tạo nghệ thuật. Rất mong các nghệ sỹ họa sỹ Việt Nam cùng tổ chức một không gian giao lưu hoc hỏi, trao đổi qua những tác phẩm, giới thiệu xa gần làm nên một sân chơi tranh thực sự ấn tượng và đáng xem trên mạng xã hội dành cho người Việt Nam. Các bạn hãy chia sẻ trang và add thêm tất cả những người bạn yêu thích hội họa của mình vào VAS bằng cách vào trang VAS, phần ở đầu trang ghi chữ "add member" hay "thêm thành viên", bạn nhấn chuột vào đó và chọn những người bạn bạn thích giới thiệu họ về VAS và nhấn chuột. Các họa sỹ lưu ý, để được duyệt cần phải có những điều kiện sau: Tranh chụp chất lượng đẹp, không có khung bo viền đen, trắng hay khung tranh nói chung Không gửi nhiều hơn một tranh một ngày nếu không cùng là một bộ tranh không thể tách rời Ghi rõ thông tin về tranh và tên tác giả gồm có: tên tranh, kích thước, năm vẽ, chất liệu, tên tác giả Tranh phải do họa sỹ tự sáng tác không có sao chép, bất cứ họa sỹ nào vi phạm bản quyền khi được phát hiện sẽ bị block trên trang. Các họa sỹ có albumn riêng giới thiệu tranh của mình đều cần có ít nhất 20 tác phẩm đã được đăng trên VAS, albumn được mở trong mục Photo - Albumn của VAS. Tranh được đăng trong albumn đều là tranh đã được giới thiệu trên trang. Sau khi có albumn, cứ 10 tranh đã đăng sẽ được bạn update vào albumn một lần. Tranh của bạn không được duyệt có thể vì chưa đủ đáp ứng những điều kiện ở trên, ngoài ra có thể tranh chưa đạt chất lượng thẩm mỹ của trang. Hãy để Vietnam Art Space là nơi tranh Việt tỏa sáng! --------------------------------------------------------- Vietnam Art Space (VAS) enables professional artists and art lovers to connect and come closer to Vietnamese arts, specifically those created by local Vietnamese. VAS is where different artists can meet, discuss, make friends, and network with one another, sharing different perspectives in high hopes of spreading global art trends and styles. This is a place for you to recognize touching masterpieces and artworks, inspiring you to reach new levels of creativity. Hopefully, Vietnamese artists can cooperatively organize and maintain a wonderful space to effectively boost the exchange of ideas to promote a mutual learning environment in efforts to advertise and make this page become the most wanted online place for Vietnamese art fanatics and lovers. Foreigners are allowed to be members but not allowed to post on VAS as we aim to maintain the originality of Vietnamese artworks. Vietnam Art Space - Where Vietnamese Paintings Shine! 
                </div>
               </div>

                 Los Angeles Historic Theatre Foundation
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The Los Angeles Historic Theatre Foundation (LAHTF) is a 501(c)3 non-profit organization dedicated to protecting, preserving, restoring and sustaining the operation of Southern California’s historic theatres. Website: LAHTF.org. Email: info@lahtf.org. Telephone: +1 (213) 443-6201. Group Rules: (1) All posts will be reviewed and only those that deal with the subject of historic theatres, preferably in LA County, will be considered for approval. (2) Submission of spam may result in a member's removal from the group. (3) Advertising and solicitation are not permitted; this is a non-commercial group. (4) Sharing of events, photos, updates, discoveries, and recommendations which support historic theatres, particularly in the LA County area, is strongly encouraged. (5) Etiquette: Behavior such as bullying and trolling will not be tolerated and will result in the member's remove from the group. Please be civil and respectful.

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Art ROCKS!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This page seeks to collect Rock art from all over the world--for the artists, those seeking ideas or feedback, anyone wishing to share or learn a new technique, and/or those desiring an audience beyond their local rocktastic movements. From the purest of the RAK ( Random act of kindness ) Rockers to professional artists to newbies, those offering to buy, sell, ALL are welcome. You may list prices at your discretion. We only allow rock or stone art , So please no canvas or wood or other mediums Thanks ! Please share your joy. Share your MIA’s, your finds, your rocks that were released into the wild and those you're hanging onto. Share links to your own rocking pages and YouTube tutorial videos. We don’t even mind a rocking joke now and again. Just don’t be obnoxious and over-post. GOOD: sharing a link to your local page. BAD: sharing that link on every single post. We have a ZERO tolerance for attacking, mean-spirited or threatening language. Please be respectful. Disrespectful posts will be deleted along with the poster/commenter. As administrators/moderators of this group we do not endorse nor enforce copyright laws. We are not attorneys and each artist here is fully responsible for the works they create. Please keep any discussion on this matter civil, factual and preferably private. Should you come across artwork that doesn’t rock your world, we encourage you to scroll past it. There’s never a good reason to attack an artist. Understand that less popular posts automatically sift to the bottom. By commenting in any fashion, you’re keeping the post current and on top. Should the post itself be attacking or mean-spirited, report it to the admin. Please resist the temptation to chime in. Should you come across any UNRELATED advertising, please report it to our admin. We know y’all are here for the rocks and the art and are simply just not that into seeing other things on this page. Should comments start to go sideways, tag one of us. We respectfully request that you do NOT add to the fire. We’ve only seen this happen a couple times, but felt it was worth adding a line here. Derogatory comments about the admin can be found in the circular files (trash can). This is a FB page. It’s not a government entity or an entitlement of any kind. It’s a hobby page we created for fun and inspiration. While we feel this belongs to all of us on some level, we’re not willing to take any grief over it. Should you like to file a complaint about us or our decisions, rant, attack, threaten or insult, you will be directed to the aforementioned circular files where you’ll find your blocked membership and best wishes to find a page more suited to you. Love one another y’all. Please keep it about the art, the artist, the RAK (random act of kindness) and your connection. That's what we're here for. &lt;3 
                </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Circus Historical Society
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This Facebook group is for people who are interested in circus history. It is sponsored by the Circus Historical Society, Inc. (CHS) which is a 501c3 non-profit educational organization that was founded in 1939. The CHS is dedicated to recording the history of the American circus from the first one in Philadelphia during 1793 to today. This Facebook group is private. New members must answer each of the Membership Questions* to join this Facebook group. Discussion topics include all aspects of circus history. No advertising for the sale of merchandise is permitted. Bullying, harassment, and rudeness will not be tolerated. Members of the CHS Facebook group are encouraged to join the CHS itself. Membership includes people from all walks of life including historians, scholars, circus personnel, memorabilia collectors, Americana specialists and just folks who share both a love of the circus and a desire to preserve and disseminate its great and interesting heritage. Paid CHS membership includes a subscription to the Bandwagon magazine which is published quarterly. The Bandwagon includes scholarly articles by leading circus historians as well as historic photos and illustrations. As in most organizations that share a common interest, the CHS members gather annually at a different location in North America to hold a convention. Papers are given. Rare archival images, films and documents are displayed. Meaty tidbits of circus history are exchanged. Current circus executives set forth their views and challenges. Friendships are renewed and new ones made, all in the interest of circus history preservation. These sessions represent the culmination of a focused year of circus research and writings on the part of many CHS members and are cherished visits to the circus past and present. Contact us at CHStreasurer@gmail.com or visit our website at www.circushistory.org 
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">1.1&nbsp;万位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">10 篇新帖</span></span>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Eritrea Architectural History and Heritage
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  Eritrea Architectural History and Heritage Despite ancient roots, Asmara, the capital of Eritrea, is most famous for its 20th-century architecture. After becoming the capital of the Italian colony in the late 19th century, the city grew to become a sizable town by the 1920s. In the 1930s, the city grew substantially as tens of thousands of Italians moved to the region in preparation for Mussolini’s planned invasion of Ethiopia. In this environment, the city became a kind of experimenting ground for modern architectural designs. Thousands of buildings were built in various styles, including Futurist, Novocento, Rationalist, and Art Deco, part of the grand city plan that also included boulevards and wide sidewalks.. The majority of the structures in the historic core date from 1935 to 1941, by which time Asmara was the main city of Mussolini’s empire in Africa. Some of the best examples of the bold, whimsical Modernist structures include the aircraft-inspired Fiat Tagliero gas station built in 1938 with a freestanding concrete cantilever roof, and the Cinema Impero, built in 1937 with a circuit-board-inspired facade. The buildings in the historic core of Asmara have remained relatively untouched since the 1940s. Intermittent unrest between Mussolini’s defeat in Africa and independence in 1991 prevented large-scale construction in the capital. Following independence in 1991, the government of Eritrea established a program to preserve this unique architectural heritage among pressures to resume development. After being listed on the Watch in 2006, the city center of Asmara received a wealth of international attention, and with assistance from the World Bank, the government established a Historic Perimeter to protect the architectural heritage. Shortly afterward, Asmara’s early Modernist architecture was featured in a traveling exhibition and workshop, a documentary film on its architectural merits, and a number of high profile travel articles featuring this preserved urban landscape. Although a comprehensive catalog of the most important buildings in town was created, Eritrea has been unable to continue its progress in the development of guidelines for the management of its architectural heritage and so far this is no finalized master plan for the conservation of the historic core of the city. Asmara represents one of the most concentrated and intact assemblages of Modernist architecture anywhere in the world. UNESCO World Heritage Site, the urban design within the Historic Perimeter has remained untouched since its original implementation and subsequent evolution throughout the 1930s. The buildings are superlative examples of various styles of Modern architecture in a preserved urban landscape. 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Mosaic Mentoring
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 PLEASE ANSWER ALL 3 QUESTIONS WHEN ASKING TO JOIN MOSAIC MENTORING. Mosaic Mentoring is a positive learning environment for mosaic artists of all levels, to share information, mentor and learn about the fine art of mosaics. We screen for admission. If we can not reach you by message, we can not accept you. So to insure that we admit you please check your other folder for a message from one of our admins. Once in the group, RULES must be read and followed. https://www.facebook.com/notes/mosaic-mentoring/welcome-rules-please-read-first/621680207982905/ No art dealers please, and I require profile pictures for all members. If you do not have any friends in common, or are not part of any mosaic groups, someone will send you a private message to make sure that you are here to learn mosaics. This is not a place for self promotion of your art, although we do have specific times for promotions. Please refrain from posting things that are not mosaic related. Hosted by Karen Sasine, a professional member of SAMA, The Society of American Mosaic Artists. My goal is to provide valuable content and mentoring to the mosaic community in a positive, helpful environment. The Admins that assist me in running the group are Jacque Towner, Kim Immenhausen Kelly, Lisa Garchow, Heather Robinson, Anitra Duke, Alicia Ortiz, Amy Struzzieri, Lisa Stakoff Skibenes and Cyndi Gilstrap McDonnough. My admins and I try to monitor most of the posts, but sometime we miss a few. Please tag my admins or myself in a post if you would like to ask me a question personally. I welcome you with open arms to this wonderfully gifted community, and invite you to share your knowledge and passion of mosaics. For the love of mosaics, Karen Sasine

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 "En Plein Air" Paintings and Painters.
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 No more than four images during each week...different days. More than one image can be in each posting. Most artists know "Plein Air" is a French term meaning to paint outside on location. This means "in the open air". The Impressionists were known for painting out in the open air. This type of painting can be traced back into the 1800's. This group site is to bring together the modern day "En Plein Air" painter. Plein air painting has continued to increase in popularity.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 +Socialist Modernism group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Constructions or buildings designed in spirit of socialist architecture (1955-1991) and the aesthetics forms of those socialist modernist years which have become this days increasingly popular among experts and not only. Socialist modernism is an approach to architecture that was typical to the former socialist countries between 1955 and 1991 and was insufficiently covered by architecture history. The modernist trend was officially adopted as a result of historical events. 1955 was the official moment when ‟useless stylistic elements” in architecture were abandoned, by decision of the Central Committee of the U.S.S.R. Communist Party. From there on, Stalinist (or realist-socialist) architecture was replaced throughout the socialist bloc. For some background into the Socialist Modernism phenomena, please refer to this webpages: socialistmodernism.com/ socialistmodernism.com/about romd.socialistmodernism.com/ . . soc-monumental art associated to soc-modernism: socmonumentalart.com/ 
                </div>
               </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Identify and value my paintings
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 "Identifying with a little help from your friends". Description: "Social Learning" Art Research Group. Members share their knowledge and work as a team to try and identify the origin of unknown works of art. "Identify MY Paintings", means you must own the art posted, not a clients, employers or one for sale elsewhere. This is not a group to critique self created works of art. The main focus is on paintings, may include other visual art forms of drawings, sculptures, prints from various printmaking techniques &amp; frames. Members have a very diverse background. Although many members in the group have degrees, others have years of life experience in the field, some members love the research others are just learning with only a desire to help. On ID requests, you are asking for opinions, thoughts &amp; ideas of all our members. We encouraged everyone to participate as it is part of the learning process. Be kind to those trying to help. Choose to "Ignore rather then Engage" troublemakers. Report to admin if need be. Any valuations given are the sole opinion of the person giving the valuation using their experience, knowledge and art market sales. These valuations are not binding or for use for insurance or other purposes, but meant as useful or helpful opinion as to value. (See Unit 1 for Appraisal information.) Any comments made do not necessarily reflect the opinion of the Admins. Some of "Our team" and their diverse background: Members introductions. https://www.facebook.com/groups/iavmp/permalink/1369236109853913/ Please, do not post in this group for identification help if you can not provide the basics requested below, leave your post for others to learn by, for admins use, or if you can not wait two weeks before attempting to sell. Own what you post. *Basics to post for Id &amp; signature help. One work per post, (unless by the same artist) two works per day. Post three images (more if needed), full front, full verso (back), a closeup of any marks or signature. If you do not see a signature take a close detailed picture of the surface texture. Provide the area the work was acquired and the measurements. Limited self promotion is allowed at designated places ONLY. (Units (Learning Tab) - Unit 1 - See Poll and designated areas.) It is treated as un-welcomed SPAM anywhere else. This is not a Trade group, members should refrain from asking if art is for sale or saying it is or will be for sale. When posting leave off mentioning your business name or charities. For add'l help, see Files "Welcome - Your guide to getting started: https://www.facebook.com/groups/iavmp/learning_content/?filter=232317940971637 Group related questions may be asked at "Check In - Artwork posting instructions", no PM's to Creator/admin. Note:Those blocking Admins will be removed. We reserve the right to remove any member at any time. Grammar and Spell check police are awarded the title of "Captain". toot toot.
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Burlesque
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 For those with an interest in all things Burlesque. Burlesque is a style of live entertainment that encompasses pastiche, parody, and wit. The genre traditionally encompasses a variety of acts such as dancing girls, chanson singers, comedians, mime artists, and strip tease artistes, all satirical and with a saucy edge. In the 50s the strip tease element of burlesque became subject to extensive local legislation, leading to a theatrical form that titillated without falling foul of censors. Please use this group to alert people to performances, events, costumiers and so on.

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Aloha Kakou, Malo e lelei, Talofa lava and Bula (Greetings to all). This is a site dedicated to the Polynesian (Tahitian, Samoan, Rapanui, Maori, Marquesan and Hawaiian) communities around the world or other nationalities who have a love for the tattoo artwork that mean so much to the wearer whether it means protection, family, loved ones or achievements. They are very personal and should not be copied. Please load up your pictures and stories behind these tattoos, and feel free to talk about the tattoo tradition. Enjoy.                  “Architecture is the learned game, correct and magnificent, of forms assembled in the light.”....Le Corbusier "Architecture is a beautiful thing to love | and an even better thing to share" Architecture is the mother of the arts, it is the thing that makes all other arts possible like wall paintings and things like that; they have to be in an architectural setting all day. -Philip Johnson- Dear friends. Please only use this group to post and comment on issues of architecture, engineering, art, urbanism, design and nature protection. As stated in our rules, this space should not be used: To send a negative context pornography, advertising a commercial company or products. We really appreciate and thankful to those of you who have sent things as per our rules. Best of luck all of you. Thank you.

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Fun with Acrylic Painting
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 GROUP RULES To join you must answer the questions provided when joining. If you don't answer them, we will not admit you into the group. 1. NO SELLING, ADVERTISING, FUNDRAISING OR PROMOTING OF ANY KIND. Listing stores having art supply sales or free supplies to give away is allowed. Free online or in-person classes is allowed, MUST BE FREE CLASSES) 2. We accept ALL forms of VISUAL ART created by YOU and skill levels. If the work was inspired by someone else, please state the artist, website, or where it came from. 3. We are an all ages group (13+) 4. NUDE, RELIGIOUS AND POLITICAL ARTWORK IS ALLOWED (NO sexual acts or nude children permitted). We do not censor art unless it breaks a direct rule noted in brackets. 5. Do not post more than 3 single images a day, group them in one post please. 6. Art posts only 7. We have a monthly contest for all to join, check the pinned post for more details as the theme changes. The entries are posted anonymously by an admin so voting is fair. The winner with the most votes becomes our monthly group image and chooses the next month's theme. 8. ZERO TOLERANCE FOR: Rudeness towards admins or members Harassment towards admins or members Racism/Religious/Gender attacks Arguing with members/admin. Bullying If you like or comment agreeing with a rude/harrassing/bullying comment you will be removed from the group. 9. Critiquing is only allowed when the artist asks for feedback. ONLY Positive critiques please. Example: Question: "how can I make my painting more life-like?" Answer: "try adding highlights and shadowing. if you'd like help I can show you what I mean" 10. Do not post your work in someone else's post unless asked to do so. 11. Report any posts you find that break our rules or Facebook's by reporting it to the admin team or tagging us in the post. Do not take matters into your own hands. If you dislike someone or their posts but they are allowed, hide their posts from your newsfeed or block them personally (do not block admins though) 12. If you block any of the listed admins, you will be removed from the group. Adaya Adalay Aurina Counts-Garbovits Pooja Verma Allison AR Lastly the name says "Fun" so that's what we ask that we all have here :) enjoy the group and Welcome to our artist family. 
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Painting Tips, Tricks, And Inspiration!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 *This group is more helpful if you use the search bar. type is keys words such as "tutorials", "tips", "paint brushes"... Go to the albums section and see if there is anything that is useful to you. A lot of members share their paintings, and this sometimes frustrates people because they thought this group is only a "tips and tricks" type group. We encourage everyone to post finished paintings and work in progress paintings. A picture could be all the inspiration someone needs. Not all tips and tricks need to be about explaining something. ☺️ Please share any tips, tricks, tutorials, or any ideas, inspiration or anything that motivates you! Keep it positive and ask questions. There is no right or wrong way to do anything, but there is always a different way right?! So let’s give our best suggestions and tips. Have fun and paint on! (or rock on 🤘 whatever your choice may be!) Please post any pictures of rocks or canvases you have recently painted. A picture can be all the motivation someone needs. This group does not allow any selling of rocks, but you may post a link to your page in the comments :) Check out the albums, I'll be adding helpful tips there. This group is for all kinds of painting. Rocks, canvases, wood, ornaments, if you can paint it then post it! If it can be done on a canvas then it can be done on a rock, or paper, or an ornament. Post pictures of work in progress and give helpful tips or something you learned while painting your last piece.. Check out the albums section. I will create albums (instead of files) for helpful tips. Also feel free to create your own album with your personal work in it. Thanks for joining us, I hope we can learn a lot from each other! Not all tips and tricks are posted. If you see someones painting you like and you have questions, please ask in the comments under that painting. We do hope that questions get answered as this is a group to help each other out!
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Rock Painting Ideas &amp; Resources
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The Kindness Rock Project is a wonderful way to bring your creative juices to the surface and create rocks that bring joy to others. Show off your newest creations so others can get some inspiration from you. Here's a couple blog posts I wrote to help you get started:http://montanahappy.com/rock-painting-how-to-get-started/ and http://montanahappy.com/the-art-of-stone-painting-book-review/ Group Rules: No Political rocks - there's enough of that stuff on Facebook Family-friendly rocks only. G rated. No posts advertising other groups. Don't post rocks for sale. This is only to show off your designs and give the group new ideas. (I do post a daily rock for inspiration. Because of copyright laws I share rocks that I find for sale on Etsy. I'm not directing people to buy them - just use them for inspiration. None of the rocks I share from Etsy are mine or anyone I know.) Please make sure you don't take rocks from National Parks and local businesses. The business owners have to pay for the rocks for their landscaping. Have fun! 
                </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Women Artists &amp; their Art. Post only 3 images each time.
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a group site created and dedicated to &amp; for Women Artists ONLY.. Why just women artists? Because ages ago women artists were the fire behind their artist spouses. Some of these women were also painters, but were NOT given the recognition of their male counterparts. Times have changed and have gotten far better of course, but they still in some cases, do not always get the recognition they deserve because they are not a man. So, this group site gives women artists the opportunity to shine, to show their work. ..whatever that work or their talents might be, as long as it is appropriate to this group. Could be Fine art, crafts, jewelry, photography....just as long as it looks professional...and is original work by you.. Educational posts about women art exhibitions. awards and also about women of the past may be posted. Video's of you doing your art may be posted too. Nothing Political. 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 VAUDEVILLE!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 WELCOME NEW MEMBERS!! * PLEASE NOTE: THIS GROUP CELEBRATES EARLY 20TH CENTURY. * THIS GROUP IS NOT ABOUT CONTEMPORARY VAUDEVILLE. * OFF TOPIC POSTS WILL BE REMOVED. THANKS!! Vaudeville is a theatrical genre of variety entertainment. It was especially popular in the United States and Canada from the early 1880s until the early 1930s. A typical vaudeville performance is made up of a series of separate, unrelated acts grouped together on a common bill. Types of acts have included popular and classical musicians, singers, dancers, comedians, trained animals, magicians, female and male impersonators, acrobats, illustrated songs, jugglers, one-act plays or scenes from plays, athletes, lecturing celebrities, minstrels, and movies. A vaudeville performer is often referred to as a vaudevillian. Vaudeville developed from many sources, including the concert saloon, minstrelsy, freak shows, dime museums, and literary burlesque. Called "the heart of American show business," vaudeville was one of the most popular types of entertainment in North America for several decades. http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vaudeville Stars of Vaudeville Series: http://travsd.wordpress.com/2009/04/03/stars-of-vaudeville-series/

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Watercolor Beginners &amp; Enthusiasts
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a group for watercolor beginners &amp; people who love watercolor. We discuss watercolor technique &amp; learning the medium. I want to keep this group on focus so people can learn about the medium. It is that simple. If you do not adhere to this focus, I am sorry to say I will remove posts that do not pertain to the medium. PLEASE - only WATERCOLOR artwork. This is a place for beginners to share their work, learn techniques &amp; materials and inspire each other! NO give-a-ways to promote your art. No Soliciting for work or competitions. * (update 4-29-18) No advertising to promote yourself or your company (it is ok to share products that you find helpful &amp; think our members would enjoy checking out) NO SELLING of your art. Be kind and supportive of eachother. If you are offended by a piece of art either scroll past it or report it to me. Please do not post images that may be inappropriate - profanity, politics, etc. I appreciate art expressionism, but this is a group to learn techniques. Join the Art Expressionism Beyond the Techniques Group if you want to get a response the the subjectivity. Nudity is allowed when done is tasteful manner and for learning purposes, with the depiction of the nude body in a non-sexualized manner. This means no painting depicting close ups of genitals or manipulation of genitals, sexual intercourse or depictions of physical/bodily contact suggestive of such. No depictions of violent sexual acts or fetishes involving ANY form of sexual violence inflicted to humans or animals. (https://www.facebook.com/communitystandards#nudity) Please abide by Copyright laws. Here are the basics: (also see Files / Web Resources) Copying other artists artwork - if you are learning, you can copy artists paintings BUT you cannot post them on the web, you can not sell them, you cannot claim them as yours. Basically, paint it, store it for your own knowledge. Copying photographs - same as above. You can get the photographers permission, then use as you have agreed to with photographer. Best option - use your own photos for reference or find royalty free images. There are websites listed in our Resources file. Admin has right to delete posts that are deemed inappropriate for this BEGINNER WATERCOLOR SHARING GROUP. You can report or flag posts. I have NO problem blocking and deleting inappropriate posts &amp; their posters. I don't have time to read all posts &amp; am so happy that 90% are lovely, beautiful watercolor works! History: What once was a gathering place for my watercolor students (all 20 of them) has grown to a worldwide group of watercolor beginners, experts, new to watercolor, haven't painted forever, have never painted, just want to have fun painters! Please share your watercolor techniques. New paintings. Inspiration, Tutorials, Stories &amp; love of watercolor!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Collage Artists of America
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Mixed media, assemblage, and digital collage artists are the heart and soul of Collage Artists of America (CAA). Founded in 1988, CAA is a non-profit organization with a membership of over 150 paying members, not to mention more than 8,000 members participating on Facebook. Our FB members give us insight into contemporary collage-arts all over the world. And for this we are grateful. The land-based membership (many of whom have exhibited nationally and internationally) enjoys 5 meetings per year which include renowned speakers and collaborative projects, workshops, professionally juried exhibits with cash awards, and supports an annual college student scholarship award. CAA Facebook Rules: In the collages we post: 1. Nudity is fine, but not porn as in sexually explicit imagery. 2. Depiction of violence is OK, but advocating it in any way is not. 3. Religious iconography is welcome. 4. Political imagery is also OK. If you don't share an opinion, scroll on. 5. You may post only once per day but that post may include multiple images. If you just post a link to your page or website, that will be deleted. 6. Attempts to sell art and any mention of pricing is not allowed, nor is advertising workshops/classes/exhibits that are not free. 7. Name-calling and otherwise heavy-handed snarky remarks will be deleted as will the author be warned and/or removed. When applying to be a member of this page, if questions are not answered, your request will be denied. Please advise your friends. If these rules are violated your post will be deleted and you may be blocked from this page.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Acrylic Painting For Beginners +
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 RULES: Paint! Share! Chat! Learn! Please read all of the group rules! Thank you! This group was created for those who paint with Acrylic to share their art work and learn from others. It is a support group! Simple rules: 1. Encouragement and advice always welcome! Rude and unnecessary comments will be deleted. (No explanation) Keep your language clean! (No swearing) No Drama! 2. No selling or self promotion (post will be deleted first, then you will be removed if it continues) 3. No links to follow you on any social media. (No YouTube, Instagram, # hashtags etc.) Post pictures directly to our group. Do not share from your personal page. We want to keep the feed clean and about the Art! -Exception- After you post a picture of your art work, you may post a link to a personal tutorial in the comments section of your own post. Also, anytime someone asks for it, you may post links in the comments. If you want to share a tutorial you love. Tell us about it in a post, then post the link in the comments section. -In addition please do not watermark your painting with your business, art page, etsy page, etc. Your name in water mark is fine. Also the signed painting is fine. 4. No vulgar, nude, suggestive, violent, disturbing, graphic or gory art. No inappropriate images. They will be removed with no explanation. Second time, you will be removed. (We have young members) 5. Please keep this page “Acrylic” paintings only. There are many other groups for different mediums! (Non-Acrylic posts will be removed to keep the page on topic) -A video of your painting is also fine. Please post any edited or “moving” paintings in the comment section of your post. -Please post reference photos in the designated album unless you are sharing them with your painting. -NO OIL/Acrylic Paintings (there are many Oil groups available) Thank you! -No Mixed Media 6. No Crafts. This includes but is not excluded to: furniture, vases, jars, plates, ornaments, pots, 3d objects etc. (At the discretion of Admin/Mods) Exception: Rocks, windows, walls, wood planks 7. No Political or Personal Agenda messages. 8. No Drugs, Alcohol, or Smoking of any kind in your ART or TALK. (Family Friendly) 9. Must give credit to original artist. Thank you!
